 			fx: {
 				opacity: "toggle",

 			},
 			create: function (event, ui) {
 				$('.ui-corner-top', this).removeClass('ui-corner-top');
 			},
 			hide: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			show: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			activate: function (event, ui) {
 				var sliderClassName = ui.newPanel.attr('id');
 				if ( sliderClassName.indexOf("fragment-ad") > -1 ) {
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb .nfy-arrow-left").hide();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb .nfy-arrow-right").hide();
 				}
 				else {
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb .nfy-arrow-left").show();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb .nfy-arrow-right").show();
 				}
 			}
 		});
 
 		counter_5b5ef21150bfb = 0;
 		autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b5ef21150bfb = true;
 		max_index_5b5ef21150bfb = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function () {
 					if ( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' ) {
 						return true;
 					}
 					return false;
 				}).length) - 1;
 
 		requestInterval(function () {
 			if ( counter_5b5ef21150bfb > max_index_5b5ef21150bfb * 10 ) {
 				counter_5b5ef21150bfb = counter_5b5ef21150bfb % (max_index_5b5ef21150bfb + 1);
 			}
 
 			if ( autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b5ef21150bfb ) {
 				max_index_5b5ef21150bfb = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function () {
 							if ( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' ) {
 								return true;
 							}
 							return false;
 						}).length) - 1;
 
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb").tabs("option", "active", ++counter_5b5ef21150bfb % (max_index_5b5ef21150bfb + 1));
 			}
 		}, 10000);
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb .nfy-arrow-right").click(function () {
 			$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb").tabs("option", "active", (++counter_5b5ef21150bfb % (max_index_5b5ef21150bfb + 1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb .nfy-arrow-left").click(function () {
 			$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb").tabs("option", "active", (--counter_5b5ef21150bfb % (max_index_5b5ef21150bfb + 1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb").swipe({
 			excludedElements: "button, input, select, textarea, .noSwipe",
 			swipeLeft: function () {
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb").tabs("option", "active", (++counter_5b5ef21150bfb % (max_index_5b5ef21150bfb + 1)));
 			},
 			swipeRight: function () {
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21150bfb").tabs("option", "active", (--counter_5b5ef21150bfb % (max_index_5b5ef21150bfb + 1)));
 			},
 			allowPageScroll: 'vertical'
 		});
 	});

 			/*heightStyle: "auto",*/
 			event: "mouseover",
 			fx:{
 				opacity: "toggle",
 				duration: "medium"
 			},
 			create: function(event, ui) {
 				$('.ui-corner-top', this).removeClass('ui-corner-top');
 			},
 			hide: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			show: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			activate: function(event, ui) {
 				var sliderClassName = ui.newPanel.attr('class');
 				if( sliderClassName.indexOf("fragment--ad") > -1 )
 				{
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 .nfy-arrow-left").hide();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 .nfy-arrow-right").hide();
 				}
 				else
 				{
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 .nfy-arrow-left").show();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 .nfy-arrow-right").show();
 				}
 			}
 		});
 
 		counter_5b5ef21824887 = 0;
 		autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b5ef21824887 = true;
 		max_index_5b5ef21824887 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function() {
 			if( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' )
 			{
 				return true;
 			}
 			return false;
 		}).length)-1;
 
 		requestInterval(function() {
 			if( counter_5b5ef21824887 > max_index_5b5ef21824887 * 10 )
 			{
 				counter_5b5ef21824887 = counter_5b5ef21824887 % (max_index_5b5ef21824887+1);
 			}
 
 			if(autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b5ef21824887)
 			{
 				max_index_5b5ef21824887 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function() {
 					if( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' )
 					{
 						return true;
 					}
 					return false;
 				}).length)-1;
 
 				$( "#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887" ).tabs( "option", "active", ++counter_5b5ef21824887 % (max_index_5b5ef21824887+1));
 			}
 		}, 10000);
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 .nfy-arrow-right").click(function() {
 			$( "#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887" ).tabs( "option", "active", (++counter_5b5ef21824887 % (max_index_5b5ef21824887+1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887 .nfy-arrow-left").click(function() {
 			$( "#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887" ).tabs( "option", "active", (--counter_5b5ef21824887 % (max_index_5b5ef21824887+1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887").swipe({
 			excludedElements: "button, input, select, textarea, .noSwipe",
 			swipeLeft: function() {
 				$( "#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887" ).tabs( "option", "active", (++counter_5b5ef21824887 % (max_index_5b5ef21824887+1)));
 			},
 			swipeRight: function() {
 				$( "#nfy-cobo-5b5ef21824887" ).tabs( "option", "active", (--counter_5b5ef21824887 % (max_index_5b5ef21824887+1)));
 			},
 			allowPageScroll: 'vertical'
 		});
 	});
